The output will include a detailed explanation of the reasoning steps taken to arrive at the final verdict. The system will also perform consistency checks to ensure that the verdict aligns with existing knowledge and will not follow common templates used in previous evaluations.\n\nStatements will be evaluated based on the following criteria:\n1. Credibility of the source.\n2. Accuracy of numerical or factual claims.\n3. Alignment with established facts.\n4. Consistency with other verified information.\n\nIf the statement cannot be confidently verified or contradicts reliable information, it will be labeled as "False." In cases where there is significant uncertainty, the system will indicate this through a lower confidence score, but will still provide a reasoned verdict based on available evidence.\n</ANSWER>']
